Psilotum nudum (L.) Beauv.	PSILOTACEAE\n松葉蕨\nAerial stems green, erect or pendent, 10-50 cm long, angular; leaves awl-shaped, 1-2 mm long. Widely distributed in tropics and subtropics. Terrestrial or more often epiphytic; small plants usuall erect; large plants pendent.\n\nTAIPEI: Tatungshan, Kuo 2334*. IISINCHU: Manabashan, Do 725. NANTOU: Chingshuikou, Huang 1940.\nPINGTUNG: Nanjenshan, Kao 73440. TAITUNG: Tawu, Chuang 3461; Is. Lanyu, Huang & Kao 5458.\nHUALIEN: Chingshuishan, Nakamura 3578.

松葉蕨	nPsilotum nudum (L.) Beauv., Prodr. Fam. Aetheog. 112. 1805; DeVol in Fl. Taiwan 1: 25. 1975. 松葉蕨\nPSILOTACEAE(松葉蕨科)\nAerial stems green, erect or pendent, 10-50 cm long, angular; leaves awl-shaped, 1-2 mm long. Widely distributed in tropics and subtropics. Terrestrial or more often epiphytic; small plants usuall erect; large plants pendent.\n\nTAIPEI: Tatungshan, Kuo 2334*. IISINCHU: Manabashan, Do 725. NANTOU: Chingshuikou, Huang 1940.\nPINGTUNG: Nanjenshan, Kao 73440. TAITUNG: Tawu, Chuang 3461; Is. Lanyu, Huang & Kao 5458.\nHUALIEN: Chingshuishan, Nakamura 3578.

Psilotaceae	松葉蕨科\nDEVOL, CHARLES E. and SHIEH, WANG-CHUENG\nVascular plants without roots; stems erect or pendent, dichotomously or unbranched; rhizomes mycorrhizal, with a protostele; aerial stem with a siphonostele. Leaves scale-like, lacking midrib, or elliptical with midrib. Sporangia borne in axils of leaves, 2-3 lobed, eusporangiate, homosporous. Gametophyte subterranean, cylindrical, mycorrhizal.\nTwo living genera, one in Taiwan.\nPsilotum nudum (L.) Beauv., Prodr. Fam. Aetheog. 112. 1805; DeVol in Fl. Taiwan 1: 25. 1975. 松葉蕨
